<P STYLE="font: 14pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center"><B>Walmart&rsquo;s Global Compliance Program</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 14pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center"><B>Report on Fiscal Year 2015</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center; border-bottom: Black 2px solid">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: center">&nbsp;</P>

<DIV STYLE="float: left; position: relative; width: 60%">

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: left">At Walmart, we are committed to ethics, compliance, and doing business the right way.</P>

<P STYLE="margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 0; text-align: left">I am pleased to share our second
annual report on our global compliance program. This report highlights significant strides we&rsquo;re making to elevate our
compliance program globally. I&rsquo;m proud of these accomplishments, as they advance our never-ending mission to ensure the
trust of our customers, associates and shareholders.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 3in 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 3in 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left"><B>Doug McMillon</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">President and CEO, Wal-Mart Stores, Inc.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left"><I>April 22, 2015</I></P>

</DIV>

<DIV STYLE="float: right; position: relative; width: 39%">

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 20pt 0pt 0; text-align: right"><IMG SRC="lwmt_photoofdougmcmillon.jpg" ALT=""></P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left"><BR CLEAR="ALL"></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 9pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-align: center">Walmart&rsquo;s Global Compliance Program &ndash; Report on Fiscal Year 2015</P>

    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 10pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; padding-bottom: 12pt; border-bottom: Silver 4px solid"><TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif"><TR><TD STYLE="text-align: center; width: 100%"><!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo -->1<!-- Field: /Sequence --></TD></TR></TABLE></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="page-break-before: always; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 10pt"><TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><TR><TD STYLE="text-align: left; width: 100%"><PAGE></PAGE></TD></TR></TABLE></DIV>




<P STYLE="font: 12pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left"><B>Building on our Progress</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">In fiscal year 2014 (FY14), Walmart devoted
significant resources to build the framework of our enhanced compliance program with the goal of operating a consistent, unified
program around the globe. Last year&rsquo;s report highlighted several structural changes to the company&rsquo;s compliance function,
summarized the expansion of Walmart&rsquo;s global compliance team and identified areas in which Walmart instituted new or improved
procedures and systems to promote compliance throughout our business.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Walmart&rsquo;s FY14 report measured progress
against a prioritized list of compliance-related enhancements our senior management developed in close coordination with the Audit
Committee of the company&rsquo;s Board of Directors. The objectives reflected careful thinking about how to build a structure that
would not only immediately enhance the company&rsquo;s compliance efforts, but also enable a cycle of continuous self-assessment
and improvement in the years to come.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">For FY15 (which ended January 31, 2015), senior
management again worked with the Audit Committee to analyze data about the company&rsquo;s risks and develop a list of prioritized
objectives to guide the global compliance organization&rsquo;s continuing efforts. The work from FY14 enabled and improved that
priority-setting process. For example, in FY14 the company recruited a number of experts in various disciplines to work in our
U.S., International, and eCommerce businesses. With these experts in place, the process for identifying, analyzing and prioritizing
compliance risks for FY15 was even more thorough and informed.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Through this process, senior management and
the Audit Committee agreed on 72 compliance objectives to be accomplished during FY15. As in FY14, the Board&rsquo;s Compensation,
Nominating and Governance Committee (&ldquo;CNGC&rdquo;) conditioned a portion of the compensation for the company&rsquo;s most
senior executives on the company making adequate progress in achieving these objectives. Under the oversight of the Audit Committee
and CNGC, the company assigned each objective to one or more senior executives to oversee, based on which executives&rsquo; areas
of authority related to each objective.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">As in FY14, our senior management reported
regularly to the Audit Committee and CNGC on the status of these objectives throughout the year. By the conclusion of FY15, the
company completed 70 of the 72 objectives and partially accomplished the remaining two. Senior management recommended that work
on the goals of the remaining two objectives be carried into the current fiscal year. In light of these results, the Audit Committee
and CNGC concluded the company made adequate progress in achieving the objectives, and did not elect to exercise the option to
reduce our executives&rsquo; compensation. For additional discussion of this topic, please see pages 52-53 of our 2015 proxy statement.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Just as these annual objectives built on the
work we accomplished the year before, this report picks up where last year&rsquo;s left off. It provides an overview of the company&rsquo;s
work to develop our compliance program over the last fiscal year through examples of the projects we undertook. As we identified,
selected and worked on the objectives, we grouped them into three top-level categories: People, Policies and Processes, and Systems
and Analytics. This report follows the same structure.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-align: center">Walmart&rsquo;s Global Compliance Program &ndash; Report on Fiscal Year 2015</P>


    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 10pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; padding-bottom: 12pt; border-bottom: Silver 4px solid"><TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif"><TR><TD STYLE="text-align: center; width: 100%"><!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo -->2<!-- Field: /Sequence --></TD></TR></TABLE></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="page-break-before: always; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 10pt"><TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><TR><TD STYLE="text-align: left; width: 100%"><PAGE></PAGE></TD></TR></TABLE></DIV>



<P STYLE="font: 12pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left"><B>People</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Over the last few years, our senior executives
and compliance professionals have examined the core areas of risk in our business and used that information to focus our compliance
program efforts. In each of our markets, our compliance program addresses at least 14 key subject matters:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left"></P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0pt; width: 99%"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 25pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 10pt; text-align: left">&bull;</TD><TD>Anti-corruption</TD>
</TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 0.25in; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

</TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 0.25in; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0pt; width: 99%"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 25pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 10pt; text-align: left">&bull;</TD><TD>Responsible sourcing</TD>
</TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 0.25in; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Each market may add topics to the program based
on risks specific to that market. Once we identified these compliance topics, the company in FY14 hired or named a global Subject
Matter Leader in each of these 14 areas to provide top-level expertise and to help maintain consistently high standards across
our business units.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">The next step, accomplished in FY15, was to
hire and realign additional compliance staff to round out our market-level compliance teams. This process included recruiting additional
staff and clearly allocating responsibilities among our compliance teams to address the 14 subject matters in our Walmart U.S.
and international businesses. It also included developing training programs to ensure our compliance associates apply the latest
developments and innovations in their field.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">While these efforts to hire and train within
the compliance program improved our capabilities, we realize the work of the more than 2,000 associates in our formal compliance
program is only a portion of what&rsquo;s needed in our overall compliance efforts if we are to succeed. It also is important to
give our associates the training, tools and support they need to serve our customers in the right way. So in FY15 we updated and
extended our compliance training programs. These enhancements are discussed in greater detail below. Additionally, recognizing
the key role our company leaders play in shaping our culture and in teaching behaviors, we revised our evaluation processes for
a number of key leadership positions to more clearly include compliance matters.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Walmart has a long-standing program to define
and promote ethical behavior. Walmart Global Ethics is responsible for promoting Walmart&rsquo;s culture of integrity. Global Ethics
is the custodian of Walmart&rsquo;s Statement of Ethics (<FONT STYLE="color: black"><U>https://walmartethics.com</U></FONT>), and
handles questions about ethical issues as well as concerns or reports of wrongdoing, among other responsibilities. Like our compliance
program, our ethics function has significantly grown and developed over the last few years. In FY15, we announced a plan to merge
Walmart&rsquo;s Ethics and Compliance programs,</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-align: center">Walmart&rsquo;s Global Compliance Program &ndash; Report on Fiscal Year 2015</P>



    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 10pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; padding-bottom: 12pt; border-bottom: Silver 4px solid"><TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif"><TR><TD STYLE="text-align: center; width: 100%"><!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo -->3<!-- Field: /Sequence --></TD></TR></TABLE></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="page-break-before: always; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 10pt"><TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><TR><TD STYLE="text-align: left; width: 100%"><PAGE></PAGE></TD></TR></TABLE></DIV>



<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">which will align Walmart with industry norms
and make our programs more effective as these teams leverage one another&rsquo;s capabilities. We expect to complete the transition
globally in FY16.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Anti-corruption is a particular area of emphasis
for our compliance program. During FY15, we continued to develop our internal anti-corruption resources. For example, we supplemented
our anti-corruption leadership team by recruiting anti-corruption directors in the eCommerce businesses at <FONT STYLE="color: black"><U>Walmart.com.br</U></FONT>
(Brazil) and <FONT STYLE="color: black"><U>Yihaodian.com</U></FONT> (China). Working with Walmart&rsquo;s global anti-corruption
team, these new directors conduct due diligence, develop and provide anti-corruption training, and oversee the implementation of
anti-corruption policies and procedures.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Also in FY14, Walmart began to appoint teams
of compliance monitors in each of our international retail markets. These monitors (known as Continuous Improvement Teams) regularly
visit our stores, assess the effectiveness of our compliance controls at store level, train our managers and associates on proper
compliance procedures, and assist the operators in correcting any issues identified. During FY15, the Continuous Improvement Team
completed over 5,500 assessments at our retail locations, identified any deviations from our policies and processes, and collaborated
with our store operators to correct over 90% of those issues by year end.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">In FY15 we expanded this concept by beginning
to carry out a multi-year plan to establish teams of compliance monitors focused on anti-corruption policies and our related financial
controls. As with the existing Continuous Improvement Teams, these monitors are designed to constantly assess and improve our performance.
We began the process of appointing these internal anti-corruption monitors in FY14 and the monitors conducted their first assessments
in FY15.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">In light of the progress in building our internal
anti-corruption capabilities, in FY15 we transitioned to our internal staff a number of activities that external consultants had
been handling. This increases the capabilities of our internal anti-corruption team, which is critical to the effectiveness and
long-term sustainability of our anti-corruption program.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left"><B>
Policies and Processes</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">
Last year&rsquo;s report noted that in FY14 our global compliance Subject Matter Leaders reviewed and revised the company&rsquo;s
global policies on each of the 14 key compliance subject matters. Building on that experience, in FY15 the company undertook a
project to review and, as necessary, revise the corresponding jurisdiction-specific procedures in each of our retail markets. As
a result, over the last two years we have taken both a global and market-specific view of our procedures and have incorporated
the most recent developments in applicable regulations.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">This process of reassessing and adjusting will
recur periodically to ensure the company&rsquo;s policies, processes and other compliance efforts remain relevant to our business
conditions. To inform the process, we conduct periodic formal compliance risk assessments. The company conducted such assessments
in FY14 and FY15. With each assessment, we are able to refine our knowledge of the issues that may affect our business and to measure
the effectiveness of our controls and other compliance measures. The information obtained during the FY15</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-align: center">Walmart&rsquo;s Global Compliance Program &ndash; Report on Fiscal Year 2015</P>





    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 10pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; padding-bottom: 12pt; border-bottom: Silver 4px solid"><TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif"><TR><TD STYLE="text-align: center; width: 100%"><!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo -->4<!-- Field: /Sequence --></TD></TR></TABLE></DIV>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">assessments also provided critical data for
senior management and our Board to use in establishing the priorities (and the formal compliance objectives) for FY16.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">In addition to refining our written policies
and procedures, we continue to devote substantial attention to training our associates through various formal and informal means.
For example, in FY14 the company designed an enhanced global anti-corruption training and communication program to further define
target audiences for anti-corruption messaging and to more effectively teach anti-corruption principles. This program came to life
over the past year in several ways, including:</P>

<TD STYLE="width: 25pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 10pt">&bull;</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: left"><FONT STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">Providing anti-corruption training to our associates
around the world in seven languages;</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 9pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</P>

<TD STYLE="width: 25pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 10pt">&bull;</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: left"><FONT STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">Enhancing the ways in which we track our anti-corruption

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Of course, anti-corruption is only one focus
of our training efforts. In FY15 we also improved our training efforts by:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0pt; width: 100%"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 25pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 10pt">&bull;</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: left"><FONT STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">Developing onboarding compliance training materials
for new associates in each of our markets; and</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 9pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0pt; width: 100%"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 25pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 10pt">&bull;</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: left"><FONT STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">Expanding our compliance training to provide
additional information for our newly promoted or hired global officers upon assuming their new positions.</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 9pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">In FY15 we also reviewed and enhanced a number
of our key compliance processes to make them more efficient and effective. These enhancements related to processes for preventing
money laundering, complying with foreign asset control regulations, and securing our licenses and permits around the globe, among
others.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">FY15 was a notable year of progress for our
global food safety program. For example, for the past 15 years, the non-governmental Global Food Safety Initiative has provided
guidance for industry-driven food-safety standards to achieve a safer global supply chain. To assess compliance with the initiative&rsquo;s
standards, third-party auditors compare companies&rsquo; practices to one or more of the initiative&rsquo;s &ldquo;recognized schemes&rdquo;&mdash;industry
standards the initiative has determined meet internationally recognized food-safety requirements. Walmart has long been a leader
in this process. In 2008, we became the first nationwide U.S. grocer to adopt the initiative&rsquo;s standards. And in FY15, our
International division more than doubled the percentage of company-owned food-production factories certified under the initiative.
These certifications</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-align: center">Walmart&rsquo;s Global Compliance Program &ndash; Report on Fiscal Year 2015</P>


    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 10pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; padding-bottom: 12pt; border-bottom: Silver 4px solid"><TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif"><TR><TD STYLE="text-align: center; width: 100%"><!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo -->5<!-- Field: /Sequence --></TD></TR></TABLE></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="page-break-before: always; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 10pt"><TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><TR><TD STYLE="text-align: left; width: 100%"><PAGE></PAGE></TD></TR></TABLE></DIV>



<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">provide our customers with assurance that the
food produced at these facilities meets the highest safety standards.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Finally, several of our FY15 objectives addressed
compliance and social responsibility in our supply chain. We value the women and men who make the products we sell at Walmart.
Over the past year, we introduced several key improvements to our Responsible Sourcing program to help factories, suppliers and
our own associates understand their roles in creating safe, positive working environments. This includes obtaining increased disclosures
from suppliers who make our private-brand products. We are using those disclosures (along with other data) to move to a risk-based
approach to auditing factories. In the last year we also revised and published enhanced fire-safety standards and comprehensive
training materials to help factories improve compliance with our standards for suppliers. Finally, we have developed partnerships
with external groups focused on worker well-being and safety, such as the Alliance for Bangladesh Worker Safety, the Coalition
of Immokalee Workers, and Stronger Together. By strengthening our internal programs and establishing partnerships to drive progress
on key industry-wide issues, we are able to make an even bigger difference for workers in our supply chain.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 12pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left"><B>Systems &amp; Analytics</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">With many retail locations and associates throughout
the world, we have a wealth of data available to help us anticipate and identify compliance risks. Efficiently collecting and utilizing
those data can be a challenge. In FY14, the company launched an ambitious effort to develop and deploy a number of global systems
to assist with this task. In FY15, the company spent more than $40 million USD carrying out this effort and made significant progress
in installing and utilizing these technologies. This included technology to:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0pt; width: 100%"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 25pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 10pt">&bull;</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: left"><FONT STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">Track the work of Walmart&rsquo;s Continuous
Improvement Teams around the globe. These teams visit our locations to monitor conditions and to provide training when necessary.
When the teams visit a location, this closed-loop system helps them document observations and follow up on prior findings.</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 9pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0pt; width: 100%"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 25pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 10pt">&bull;</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: left"><FONT STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">Conduct due diligence research on third parties
that may interact with governmental entities on our behalf. The technology, for instance, collects&nbsp;information from the third
parties about their businesses and key personnel; it then searches various databases to identify adverse news stories, litigation,
government sanctions, and politically exposed persons relating to the third parties and their key personnel.</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 9pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0pt; width: 100%"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 25pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 10pt">&bull;</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: left"><FONT STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">Deliver training in a more efficient and engaging
way. This enhanced training technology has been installed in several of our retail markets&rsquo; home offices and will be expanded
in FY16.</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 9pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0pt; width: 100%"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 25pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 10pt">&bull;</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: left"><FONT STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">Centralize the oversight of our license and
permit applications and renewals. In FY15, we extended a global license-management system into 11 of our international retail markets.
The expanded management system organizes the licensing and permitting requirements in each market, simplifies the process for applying
for licenses, and provides a single repository for documentation associated with our licensing obligations.</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 9pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-align: center">Walmart&rsquo;s Global Compliance Program &ndash; Report on Fiscal Year 2015</P>

    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 10pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; padding-bottom: 12pt; border-bottom: Silver 4px solid"><TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif"><TR><TD STYLE="text-align: center; width: 100%"><!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo -->6<!-- Field: /Sequence --></TD></TR></TABLE></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="page-break-before: always; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 10pt"><TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="width: 100%; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><TR><TD STYLE="text-align: left; width: 100%"><PAGE></PAGE></TD></TR></TABLE></DIV>



<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0pt; width: 100%"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 25pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 10pt; text-align: left"></TD><TD>Our associates now have critical licensing information at their fingertips, along with analytics to predict and prepare
                                                                            for our licensing needs.</TD>
</TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 0.5in; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin-top: 0; margin-bottom: 0pt; width: 100%"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top">
<TD STYLE="width: 25pt"></TD><TD STYLE="width: 10pt">&bull;</TD><TD STYLE="text-align: left"><FONT STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">Streamline the process of ensuring that the
food we sell is top quality and safe. For years we have used a Sustainable Paperless Auditing and Record Keeping (&ldquo;SPARK&rdquo;)
system in our U.S. stores. SPARK utilizes state-of-the-art devices to measure food temperatures and electronically track the information.
In FY15, we began a multi-year plan to expand the SPARK system to our international retail markets.</FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 9pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left"><B>Looking Down the Road</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">These examples are a subset of the company&rsquo;s
progress in addressing ethics and compliance issues in FY15. Find additional examples in Walmart&rsquo;s&rsquo; <I>Global Responsibility
Report</I>. All of these efforts are part of Walmart&rsquo;s continuing commitment to doing business the right way.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif">To
support that commitment, the company and our Board have elected to use again in FY16 the same process for setting top-level compliance
objectives.&nbsp;For this third year of setting such objectives, and following discussions of both our progress and our data on
current risks and performance, senior management proposed focusing on 40 compliance objectives to be accomplished in FY16. The
Audit Committee and CNGC approved these objectives and once again linked them to a portion of our senior executives&rsquo; compensation.
We look forward to seeing these improvements and innovations help our business flourish and our customers live better.</FONT></P>

<P STYLE="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; font: 9pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; text-align: center">Walmart&rsquo;s Global Compliance Program &ndash; Report on Fiscal Year 2015</P>
